        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer1850496823&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1850496823" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16875877260710513891">Overall I thought this was a good trilogy, but far from great.<br/><br/>The first story was the best and had the most unique scenario. One of the plot deaths towards the end felt extremely forced, but for the most part is was good.<br/><br/>Second book did some things well and some things not so much. The situation wasn't as unique. A strange encounter at the start of the story (those of you who have read the story may remember this hot and messy scene) seemed to make little sense and was never really explained, th</span>
  <span id="freeText16875877260710513891" style="display:none">Overall I thought this was a good trilogy, but far from great.<br /><br />The first story was the best and had the most unique scenario. One of the plot deaths towards the end felt extremely forced, but for the most part is was good.<br /><br />Second book did some things well and some things not so much. The situation wasn't as unique. A strange encounter at the start of the story (those of you who have read the story may remember this hot and messy scene) seemed to make little sense and was never really explained, though it was cool and I only came to that conclusion upon completion of the book. The final battle was also a rather forced scene. The secondary love interest that appeared in this book was in my opinion one of the best characters in the trilogy.<br /><br />The third book had a very different tone to it. This one had the most questionable plot decisions, but I found it had some of the best moments as well. For most this will be their least favorite and the ending was less than satisfying.<br /><br />Overall this is a fairly easy read (thank Dashner for the casual pace of the reading, a but plus in my opinion) and you'll meet some interesting characters. If you got the time, you should certainly read this trilogy.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16875877260710513891" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9769862091136132301">The concept of this series is intriguing, but unfortunately, its effectiveness is based on how suspenseful and action-packed the scenes can be. This series is definitely targeted at a younger audience who need that much constant adrenaline in order to stay interested. I would have really loved for there to be more truth discovered, rather than the confusion and life/death stakes that defines all three books. I got more out of the prequel, even though it meant discarding the main characters in or</span>
  <span id="freeText9769862091136132301" style="display:none">The concept of this series is intriguing, but unfortunately, its effectiveness is based on how suspenseful and action-packed the scenes can be. This series is definitely targeted at a younger audience who need that much constant adrenaline in order to stay interested. I would have really loved for there to be more truth discovered, rather than the confusion and life/death stakes that defines all three books. I got more out of the prequel, even though it meant discarding the main characters in order to tell some of the history. <br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_573005279" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/573005279" />
    <a title="Kelly M" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2255825-kelly-m"><img alt="Kelly M" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1379781662p2/2255825.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/573005279?book_show_action=true">Mar 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelly M" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelly M" href="/user/show/2255825-kelly-m">Kelly M</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer573005279" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8961320022442801817">As good as The Hunger Games trilogy.....definitely a page turner. Has some witty humor albeit usually via juvenile retorts but I don't consider myself high brow when it comes to comedy. Books center around the Machiavellian question, "Do the ends justify the means?" and while it clearly favors one answer over another, there is still ambiguity surrounding this moral dilemma, which creates a depth/complexity of thinking not usually found in young adult fiction. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('gkO4urYiYwERj3csa27E5B1bDtKEtyu73TP/gD5iX+gLldsTDOHHeopDv0eqDQPzfHYaGJ1mYFn1dXp06W5pZA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('iTLZCrT3JryQKn3POWi44kS7VV+wNCqFhebTELk1E2kA5LqjDjSCxwvmtaT4C3/1JZZBlanlYWetoFbkbjkl5Q==')})
  }
